validateVersions(callerName, pluginName string, endpoint string, versions []string) (*utilversion.Version, error) {\n243: \tif len(versions) == 0 {\n244: \t\treturn nil, errors.New(log(\"%s for CSI driver %q failed. Plugin returned an empty list for supported versions\", callerName, pluginName))\n245: \t}\n246: \n247: \t// Validate version\n248: \t// CSI currently only has version 0.x and 1.x (see https://github.com/container-storage-interface/spec/releases).\n249: \t// Therefore any driver claiming version 2.x+ is ignored as an unsupported versions.\n250: \t// Future 1.x versions of CSI are supposed to be backwards compatible so this version of Kubernetes will work with any 1.x driver\n251: \t// (or 0.x), but it may not work with 2.x drivers (because 2.x does not have to be backwards compatible with 1.x).\n252: \t// CSI v0.x is no longer supported as of Kubernetes v1.17 in accordance with deprecation policy set out in Kubernetes v1.13.\n253: \tnewDriverHighestVersion, err := utilversion.HighestSupportedVersion(versions)\n254: \tif err != nil {\n255: \t\treturn nil, errors.New(log(\"%s for CSI driver %q failed. None of the versions specified %q are supported. err=%v\", callerName, pluginName, versions, err))\n256: \t}\n257: \n258: \texistingDriver, driverExists := csiDrivers.Get(pluginName)\n259: \tif driverExists {\n260: \t\tif !existingDriver.highestSupportedVersion.LessThan(newDriverHighestVersion) {\n261: \t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(log(\"%s for CSI driver %q failed. Another driver with the same name is already registered with a higher supported version: %q\", callerName, pluginName, existingDriver.highestSupportedVersion))\n262: \t\t}\n263: \t}\n264: \n265: \treturn newDriverHighestVersion, nil\n266: }\n267: \n268: // DeRegisterPlugin is called when a plugin removed its socket, signaling\n269: // it is no longer available\n270: func (h The `csiDriverClient` struct implements this interface and provides methods for node-level CSI operations including `NodePublishVolume()`, `NodeUnpublishVolume()`, `NodeStageVolume()`, `NodeUnstageVolume()`, and `NodeGetInfo()`.\\n\\n**2. CSI Plugin (pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go):**\\nThe `csiPlugin` type implements the VolumePlugin, AttachableVolumePlugin, and BlockVolumePlugin interfaces. It manages CSI driver registration through the `RegistrationHandler` and provides methods like `NewMounter()`, `NewAttacher()`, `NewDetacher()`, and `NewBlockVolumeMapper()`. The `Init()` method initializes CSI node information and registers the plugin with the kubelet.\\n\\n**3. CSI Volume Attacher (pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go):**\\nThe `csiAttacher` struct implements the volume.Attacher and volume.Detacher interfaces. It provides `Attach()` and `Detach()` operations that coordinate with the attach/detach controller and update VolumeAttachment objects in the cluster.\\n\\n**4. CSI Mount Manager (pkg/volume/csi/csi_mounter.go):**\\nThe `csiMountMgr` struct implements volume.Mounter and volume.Unmounter interfaces. It handles `SetUp()` and `TearDown()` operations by invoking the CSI node plugin's `NodeStageVolume()` and `NodePublishVolume()` calls to prepare and mount volumes on the node.\\n\\n**5. CSI Block Volume Mapper (pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go):**\\nThe `csiBlockMapper` struct handles block volume operations, implementing device mount/unmount for CSI volumes that support raw block device access.\\n\\n**6. Attach/Detach Controller (pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go):**\\nThe `attachDetachController` manages volume attachment state across the cluster. It watches for pods requiring volumes and creates VolumeAttachment objects for CSI drivers that require attach operations. It reconciles the desired and actual state of volume attachments.\\n\\n**7. PersistentVolume Controller (pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go and pv_controller_base.go):**\\nThe `PersistentVolumeController` handles dynamic provisioning, binding, and deletion of persistent volumes. CSI Node Info Manager (pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go):**\\nManages CSI driver registration on the node, creating and updating CSINode objects that advertise driver capabilities, accessible topologies, and resource allocations.\\n\\n**9. CSI Node Updater (pkg/volume/csi/csi_node_updater.go):**\\nPeriodically updates CSINode allocatable information based on CSIDriver settings, enabling dynamic capacity tracking.\\n\\n**10.
